## A. Registry Overview

- **Registry no:** `117` · **word:** `peace`
- **verse_context_status:** `Complete`
- **session_b_status:** `Verse Context Reset`
- **dim_review_status:** `Complete` (version `wa-dimensionreview-instruction-v3_3-20260418.md`)

- **dimensions (registry-level):** `Relational/Social`

**Phase 1 (registry-scoped):**
- `phase1_status`: `Complete`
- `phase1_term_count`: 125  (programme-wide aggregate including XREF and historical terms — current OWNER count is 62, XREF 6)
- `phase1_verse_count`: 2764  (programme-wide aggregate; current registry verse counts shown per term in §C)

**Open flags:** 3 unresolved · **Existing session_b_findings:** 3

**Description:**

> Peace is the condition of wholeness, right relationship, and rest — the Hebrew shalom covering far more than the absence of conflict. It means completeness, prosperity, welfare, the flourishing of everything and everyone in their proper place. It is used of the end of hostilities, of the quality of a life well-lived, of the relationship between a person and God when that relationship is restored. The New Testament declares that Christ himself is our peace: through him the fundamental rupture between humanity and God is healed. Peace is the signature of the kingdom.

- **XREF sharing** — registries that own terms appearing as XREF in this registry
- **Verse co-occurrence** — same verse classified is_relevant=1 in this registry AND another (≥3 shared verses)
- **Shared anchors** — same verse appears as is_anchor=1 in this registry AND another

#### `DIM-117-002` — `DIMENSION_REVIEW`

- **status:** `pending` · **thin_evidence:** 0 · **raised:** 2026-04-08 · **term_id:** -

> The peace registry's inner-being content is unusually wide — spanning the felt inner state of rest/peace (Emotion — Positive), the inner posture of quietness before God (Moral Character/Relational Disposition), the divine giving of rest (Transformation/GOD), and God's own inner states of rest, restraint, and jealousy. Session B should examine what shalom names as an inner-being reality: is it primarily a felt state, a relational condition, a divine gift, or an eschatological reality — and how do these dimensions interrelate?

#### `DIM-117-001` — `DIMENSION_REVIEW`

- **status:** `pending` · **thin_evidence:** 0 · **raised:** 2026-04-06 · **term_id:** -

> Peace (#117) carries 15 terms with status=extracted_theological_anchor (818 active verses). These are divine names, titles, and eternal/hosts vocabulary — YHWH-Shalom, LORD of Hosts (H6635A/B, 292 verses), El Shaddai (H7706, 48 verses), Adonai (H0136, 187 verses), El Olam (H5769G/H, 273 verses), El Elyon (H5943/H5946, 14 verses), YHWH-Nissi, YHWH-Tsidkenu, YHWH-Tsidkenu (H6664H, 2 verses), sabaoth (G4519, 2 verses). See word_registry.notes for full term list.

### H.2 Open SD pointers + research flags (3)

| flag_code | label | priority | session | raised |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `SD_POINTER` | DIM-117-SD003 | MEDIUM | D | 2026-05-01 |
| `SD_POINTER` | DIM-117-SD001 | LOW | D | 2026-04-06 |
| `SD_POINTER` | DIM-117-SD002 | LOW | D | 2026-04-06 |

#### DIM-117-SD003

> Group 2508-004 (H7965G sha.lom — messianic/eschatological peace) establishes that shalom in the Hebrew prophetic corpus is constitutively identified with the person of the messianic king: Prince of Peace (Isa 9:6), He shall be their peace (Mic 5:5), upon him was the chastisement that brought us peace (Isa 53:5). This is the OT ground of the NT claim that Christ IS peace (Eph 2:14, G1515 eirene — R117 group 426-003). Session D must examine whether the he-shall-be-their-peace structure (person = peace) in the Hebrew prophetic corpus is the direct semantic antecedent of he-himself-is-our-peace in the NT — and whether this constitutes a single unified concept across both testaments that R117 shalom and eirene groups together document. Cross-registry targets: NT eirene registries (R117 own Greek groups), R130 reconciliation (Col 1:20), messianic-identity material.

#### DIM-117-SD001

> H3070 (YHWH-Yireh, YHWH-Jireh) registration anomaly: owner_registry field points to experience (#58) but this term is registered as extracted_theological_anchor in peace (#117). Requires CC investigation to confirm correct owner registry assignment before Session B begins on peace. If owner should be peace, update mti_terms.owning_registry accordingly.

#### DIM-117-SD002

> H3068G (YHWH/Yahweh) registration anomaly: owner_registry = NULL, active_verse_count = 0. This is the primary divine name; its absence of an owner registry and zero active verses is structurally unusual. May be a registration placeholder. Requires CC investigation before Session B begins on peace to confirm whether this is intentional (placeholder, handled via H3068 variants elsewhere) or an incomplete registration.

- **Judg 6:23** 🔵 (✓) *target: Peace*
  > Judg 6:23 But the Lord said to him, “ Peace be to you. Do not fear ; you shall not die .”
  - notes: Divine word at theophany — Peace be to you. Do not fear. Shalom directly counteracts inner terror in divine encounter.
- **Psa 4:8** 🔵 (✓) *target: peace*
  > Psa 4:8 In peace I will both lie down and sleep ; for you alone , O Lord , make me dwell in safety .
  - notes: In peace I will lie down and sleep — shalom as inner condition of rest and security grounded in trust in God alone.
- **Psa 119:165** 🔵 (✓) *target: peace*
  > Psa 119:165 Great peace have those who love your law ; nothing can make them stumble .
  - notes: Great peace have those who love your law; nothing can make them stumble. Shalom as the inner condition of those oriented toward God's word.
- **Isa 26:3** 🔵 (✓) *target: perfect*
  > Isa 26:3 You keep him in perfect peace whose mind is stayed on you, because he trusts in you.
  - notes: Perfect peace (shalom shalom) for the one whose mind is stayed on God because he trusts — fullest statement of peace as inner condition produced by directed trust.
- **Lam 3:17** 🔵 (✓) *target: peace*
  > Lam 3:17 my soul is bereft of peace ; I have forgotten what happiness is;
  - notes: My soul is bereft of peace — most direct statement of shalom as inner-being condition of the soul (nephesh).
- **Gen 43:23** (✓) *target: Peace*
  > Gen 43:23 He replied , “ Peace to you, do not be afraid . Your God and the God of your father has put treasure in your sacks for you. I received your money .” Then he brought Simeon out to them.
  - notes: Peace to you, do not be afraid — shalom blessing directly paired with call not to fear; addresses inner condition of the brothers.
- **1Sa 1:17** (✓) *target: peace*
  > 1Sa 1:17 Then Eli answered , “ Go in peace , and the God of Israel grant your petition that you have made to him .”
  - notes: Go in peace after prayer — Hannah came in anguish, departs in peace after divine encounter; inner state changed.
- **Psa 37:11** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Psa 37:11 But the meek shall inherit the land and delight themselves in abundant peace .
  - notes: The meek shall delight in abundant peace — shalom as the inner condition of flourishing for the meek.
- **Pro 3:2** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Pro 3:2 for length of days and years of life and peace they will add to you .
  - notes: Length of days and peace as fruit of following wisdom — shalom as inner condition produced by wise living.
- **Pro 3:17** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Pro 3:17 Her ways are ways of pleasantness , and all her paths are peace .
  - notes: All wisdom's paths are peace — shalom as the characteristic of the way of wisdom.
- **Song 8:10** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Song 8:10 I was a wall , and my breasts were like towers ; then I was in his eyes as one who finds peace .
  - notes: One who finds peace in the beloved's eyes — shalom as the inner condition of acceptance and wholeness in relationship.
- **Isa 48:18** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Isa 48:18 Oh that you had paid attention to my commandments ! Then your peace would have been like a river , and your righteousness like the waves of the sea ;
  - notes: Your peace would have been like a river — abundance of inner shalom as counterfactual fruit of obedience.
- **Isa 57:2** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Isa 57:2 he enters into peace ; they rest in their beds who walk in their uprightness .
  - notes: He enters into peace; those who walk uprightly rest in their beds — shalom as the final inner condition of the righteous.
- **Jer 8:15** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Jer 8:15 We looked for peace , but no good came; for a time of healing , but behold , terror .
  - notes: We looked for peace but no good came — the inner-being longing for shalom unfulfilled.
- **Jer 12:12** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Jer 12:12 Upon all the bare heights in the desert destroyers have come , for the sword of the Lord devours from one end of the land to the other ; no flesh has peace .
  - notes: No flesh has peace — universal absence of shalom under divine judgment.
- **Jer 14:19** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Jer 14:19 Have you utterly rejected Judah ? Does your soul loathe Zion ? Why have you struck us down so that there is no healing for us? We looked for peace , but no good came; for a time of healing , but behold , terror .
  - notes: We looked for peace — parallel to Jer 8:15, longing for shalom.
- **Jer 30:5** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Jer 30:5 “ Thus says the Lord : We have heard a cry of panic , of terror , and no peace .
  - notes: Cry of panic, terror, and no peace — absence of shalom as inner condition in distress.
- **Eze 7:25** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Eze 7:25 When anguish comes , they will seek peace , but there shall be none .
  - notes: When anguish comes they will seek peace but there shall be none — inner-being longing for shalom in distress.
- **Dan 10:19** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Dan 10:19 And he said , “O man greatly loved , fear not , peace be with you; be strong and of good courage .” And as he spoke to me, I was strengthened and said , “Let my lord speak , for you have strengthened me .”
  - notes: Fear not, peace be with you; be strong and of good courage — angelic shalom addressing Daniel's inner terror.

**Group `2508-002`** (24 verses — anchors: Num 6:26, Psa 85:8, Isa 54:10)

- **Num 6:26** 🔵 (✓) *target: peace*
  > Num 6:26 the Lord lift up his countenance upon you and give you peace .
  - notes: Aaronic blessing — the Lord give you peace. Foundational covenant-gift of shalom within the triple divine blessing.
- **Psa 85:8** 🔵 (✓) *target: peace*
  > Psa 85:8 Let me hear what God the Lord will speak , for he will speak peace to his people , to his saints ; but let them not turn back to folly .
  - notes: God will speak peace to his people, to his saints — divine speech of covenantal peace conditioned on not turning back to folly.
- **Isa 54:10** 🔵 (✓) *target: peace*
  > Isa 54:10 For the mountains may depart and the hills be removed , but my steadfast love shall not depart from you, and my covenant of peace shall not be removed ,” says the Lord , who has compassion on you.
  - notes: My covenant of peace shall not be removed — eternal unbreakable covenant of shalom.
- **Gen 28:21** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Gen 28:21 so that I come again to my father’s house in peace , then the Lord shall be my God ,
  - notes: Jacob's vow — return in peace tied to covenantal commitment ('the Lord shall be my God'). Shalom as the condition of the one under divine protection in covenant.
- **Lev 26:6** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Lev 26:6 I will give peace in the land , and you shall lie down , and none shall make you afraid . And I will remove harmful beasts from the land , and the sword shall not go through your land .
  - notes: Covenant blessing — I will give peace in the land, none shall make you afraid. Shalom as God's gift producing freedom from inner fear.
- **Num 25:12** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Num 25:12 Therefore say , ‘ Behold , I give to him my covenant of peace ,
  - notes: Covenant of peace given to Phinehas — covenantal relational peace by divine declaration.
- **1Sa 20:42** (✓) *target: peace*
  > 1Sa 20:42 Then Jonathan said to David , “ Go in peace , because we have sworn both of us in the name of the Lord , saying , ‘The Lord shall be between me and you, and between my offspring and your offspring , forever .’” And he rose and departed , and Jonathan went into the city .
  - notes: Go in peace grounded in covenant oath sworn in the Lord's name — shalom of the covenantal friendship.
- **1Ki 2:33** (✓) *target: peace*
  > 1Ki 2:33 So shall their blood come back on the head of Joab and on the head of his descendants forever . But for David and for his descendants and for his house and for his throne there shall be peace from the Lord forevermore .”
  - notes: Peace from the Lord forevermore for David's house — covenantal peace with divine origin and eternal character.
- **1Ki 22:28** (✓) *target: peace*
  > 1Ki 22:28 And Micaiah said , “ If you return in peace , the Lord has not spoken by me.” And he said , “ Hear , all you peoples !”
  - notes: Prophetic sign — return in peace would disprove Micaiah's word; shalom as a condition bearing on prophetic truth and divine authority.
- **1Ch 12:18** (✓) *target: Peace*
  > 1Ch 12:18 Then the Spirit clothed Amasai , chief of the thirty , and he said, “We are yours, O David , and with you, O son of Jesse ! Peace , peace to you, and peace to your helpers ! For your God helps you.” Then David received them and made them officers of his troops .
  - notes: Triple shalom pronounced over David grounded in 'your God helps you' — peace of the one under divine help and favour.
- **1Ch 22:9** (✓) *target: peace*
  > 1Ch 22:9 Behold , a son shall be born to you who shall be a man of rest . I will give him rest from all his surrounding enemies . For his name shall be Solomon , and I will give peace and quiet to Israel in his days .
  - notes: God's promise: I will give peace and quiet to Israel in Solomon's days. Shalom + shaqat as divine double gift.
- **2Ch 18:27** (✓) *target: peace*
  > 2Ch 18:27 And Micaiah said , “ If you return in peace , the Lord has not spoken by me.” And he said , “ Hear , all you peoples !”
  - notes: Prophetic sign — parallel to 1Ki 22:28. Return in peace as test of prophetic truth.
- **Job 25:2** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Job 25:2 “ Dominion and fear are with God; he makes peace in his high heaven .
  - notes: God makes peace in his high heaven — divine sovereignty expressed as peace-making in the heavenly realm.
- **Psa 29:11** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Psa 29:11 May the Lord give strength to his people ! May the Lord bless his people with peace !
  - notes: May the Lord bless his people with peace — divine blessing of shalom.
- **Psa 122:6** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Psa 122:6 Pray for the peace of Jerusalem ! “May they be secure who love you !
  - notes: Pray for the peace of Jerusalem — shalom of the covenant city as the object of prayer and inner orientation.
- **Isa 26:12** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Isa 26:12 O Lord , you will ordain peace for us, for you have indeed done for us all our works .
  - notes: You will ordain peace for us — God ordaining shalom as divine gift.
- **Isa 27:5** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Isa 27:5 Or let them lay hold of my protection , let them make peace with me, let them make peace with me .”
  - notes: Let them make peace with me — relational act of reconciliation/covenant peace with God.
- **Isa 54:13** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Isa 54:13 All your children shall be taught by the Lord , and great shall be the peace of your children .
  - notes: Great shall be the peace of your children — shalom of the covenant community taught by God.
- **Isa 57:19** (✓) *target: Peace*
  > Isa 57:19 creating the fruit of the lips . Peace , peace , to the far and to the near ,” says the Lord , “and I will heal him .
  - notes: Peace, peace, to the far and to the near — God's comprehensive proclamation of covenantal shalom.
- **Jer 16:5** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Jer 16:5 “For thus says the Lord : Do not enter the house of mourning , or go to lament or grieve for them, for I have taken away my peace from this people , my steadfast love and mercy , declares the Lord .
  - notes: I have taken away my peace from this people — withdrawal of divine covenantal peace as judgment.
- **Eze 34:25** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Eze 34:25 “I will make with them a covenant of peace and banish wild beasts from the land , so that they may dwell securely in the wilderness and sleep in the woods .
  - notes: Covenant of peace with my people — God's covenant of peace in the eschatological/new covenant.
- **Eze 37:26** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Eze 37:26 I will make a covenant of peace with them. It shall be an everlasting covenant with them. And I will set them in their land and multiply them, and will set my sanctuary in their midst forevermore .
  - notes: Everlasting covenant of peace — shalom as the permanent covenant condition.
- **Hag 2:9** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Hag 2:9 The latter glory of this house shall be greater than the former , says the Lord of hosts . And in this place I will give peace , declares the Lord of hosts .’”
  - notes: In this place I will give peace — God's gift of shalom in the temple, covenantal/eschatological.
- **Mal 2:5** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Mal 2:5 My covenant with him was one of life and peace , and I gave them to him. It was a covenant of fear , and he feared me. He stood in awe of my name .
  - notes: Covenant of life and peace given to Levi — covenantal shalom as God's specific gift in priestly covenant.

**Group `2508-003`** (25 verses — anchors: Psa 120:7, Mal 2:6)

- **Psa 120:7** 🔵 (✓) *target: peace*
  > Psa 120:7 I am for peace , but when I speak , they are for war !
  - notes: I am for peace (ani shalom) — shalom as personal identity and fundamental disposition; most direct statement of peace as inner orientation.
- **Mal 2:6** 🔵 (✓) *target: peace*
  > Mal 2:6 True instruction was in his mouth , and no wrong was found on his lips . He walked with me in peace and uprightness , and he turned many from iniquity .
  - notes: He walked with me in peace and uprightness — shalom as the character of Levi's life before God; the peaceful disposition of the faithful priest.
- **Gen 37:4** (✓) *target: peacefully*
  > Gen 37:4 But when his brothers saw that their father loved him more than all his brothers , they hated him and could not speak peacefully to him.
  - notes: Brothers could not speak peaceably to Joseph — shalom names the relational-inner orientation of peace that hatred makes impossible.
- **2Ki 9:22** (✓) *target: peace*
  > 2Ki 9:22 And when Joram saw Jehu , he said , “Is it peace , Jehu ?” He answered , “ What peace can there be, so long as the whorings and the sorceries of your mother Jezebel are so many ?”
  - notes: What peace can there be while Jezebel's whorings and sorceries continue — peace explicitly conditioned on moral/spiritual fidelity; moral corruption makes peace impossible.
- **Est 10:3** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Est 10:3 For Mordecai the Jew was second in rank to King Ahasuerus , and he was great among the Jews and popular with the multitude of his brothers , for he sought the welfare of his people and spoke peace to all his people .
  - notes: Mordecai sought the welfare (shalom) of his people and spoke peace to them — shalom as inner disposition of care expressed in leadership.
- **Psa 28:3** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Psa 28:3 Do not drag me off with the wicked , with the workers of evil , who speak peace with their neighbors while evil is in their hearts .
  - notes: Speak peace with neighbors while evil is in their hearts — shalom as the false relational disposition; heart-evil contrasted with tongue-peace.
- **Psa 34:14** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Psa 34:14 Turn away from evil and do good ; seek peace and pursue it .
  - notes: Seek peace and pursue it — active pursuit of shalom as moral imperative.
- **Psa 35:20** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Psa 35:20 For they do not speak peace , but against those who are quiet in the land they devise words of deceit .
  - notes: They do not speak peace but device deceit against the quiet — shalom as the disposition absent in the wicked.
- **Psa 37:37** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Psa 37:37 Mark the blameless and behold the upright , for there is a future for the man of peace .
  - notes: The man of peace (ish shalom) has a future — shalom as personal character description.
- **Psa 120:6** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Psa 120:6 Too long have I had my dwelling among those who hate peace .
  - notes: Too long among those who hate peace — shalom as an orientation that can be hated.
- **Pro 12:20** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Pro 12:20 Deceit is in the heart of those who devise evil , but those who plan peace have joy .
  - notes: Those who plan peace have joy — shalom planning as heart-disposition producing joy; contrasted with evil in the heart.
- **Isa 32:17** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Isa 32:17 And the effect of righteousness will be peace , and the result of righteousness , quietness and trust forever .
  - notes: The effect of righteousness will be peace — shalom as fruit of righteous character orientation.
- **Isa 48:22** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Isa 48:22 “There is no peace ,” says the Lord , “ for the wicked .”
  - notes: There is no peace for the wicked — shalom impossible for those in moral disorder.
- **Isa 57:21** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Isa 57:21 There is no peace ,” says my God , “ for the wicked .”
  - notes: No peace for the wicked — parallel to 48:22.
- **Isa 59:8** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Isa 59:8 The way of peace they do not know , and there is no justice in their paths ; they have made their roads crooked ; no one who treads on them knows peace .
  - notes: The way of peace they do not know — peace as a way of life unknown to those in moral disorder.
- **Jer 6:14** (✓) *target: Peace*
  > Jer 6:14 They have healed the wound of my people lightly , saying , ‘ Peace , peace ,’ when there is no peace .
  - notes: Crying Peace, peace when there is no peace — moral violation of false peace proclamation.
- **Jer 8:11** (✓) *target: Peace*
  > Jer 8:11 They have healed the wound of my people lightly , saying , ‘ Peace , peace ,’ when there is no peace .
  - notes: Parallel to Jer 6:14 — false peace proclamation.
- **Jer 9:8** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Jer 9:8 Their tongue is a deadly arrow ; it speaks deceitfully ; with his mouth each speaks peace to his neighbor , but in his heart he plans an ambush for him.
  - notes: Speaks peace with mouth but plans ambush in heart — parallel to Psa 28:3, heart contrasted with tongue.
- **Jer 14:13** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Jer 14:13 Then I said : “ Ah , Lord God , behold , the prophets say to them, ‘You shall not see the sword , nor shall you have famine , but I will give you assured peace in this place .’”
  - notes: False prophets promising assured peace — false peace promise.
- **Jer 28:9** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Jer 28:9 As for the prophet who prophesies peace , when the word of that prophet comes to pass , then it will be known that the Lord has truly sent the prophet .”
  - notes: The prophet who prophesies peace — the prophetic test of peace proclamation; truth demonstrated by fulfilment.
- **Eze 13:10** (✓) *target: Peace*
  > Eze 13:10 Precisely because they have misled my people , saying , ‘ Peace ,’ when there is no peace , and because, when the people build a wall , these prophets smear it with whitewash ,
  - notes: Saying Peace when there is no peace — false prophets; moral corruption of the peace proclamation.
- **Eze 13:16** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Eze 13:16 the prophets of Israel who prophesied concerning Jerusalem and saw visions of peace for her, when there was no peace , declares the Lord God .
  - notes: Saw visions of peace for her when there was no peace — false prophetic visions.
- **Mic 3:5** (✓) *target: Peace*
  > Mic 3:5 Thus says the Lord concerning the prophets who lead my people astray , who cry “ Peace ” when they have something to eat , but declare war against him who puts nothing into their mouths .
  - notes: Prophets cry Peace for payment — moral corruption of the peace proclamation for gain.
- **Zec 8:16** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Zec 8:16 These are the things that you shall do : Speak the truth to one another ; render in your gates judgments that are true and make for peace ;
  - notes: Render judgments that make for peace — peace as the telos of just governance, requiring intentional orientation.
- **Zec 8:19** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Zec 8:19 “ Thus says the Lord of hosts : The fast of the fourth month and the fast of the fifth and the fast of the seventh and the fast of the tenth shall be to the house of Judah seasons of joy and gladness and cheerful feasts . Therefore love truth and peace .
  - notes: Love truth and peace — shalom as the object of love, a disposition of the heart.

**Group `2508-004`** (15 verses — anchors: Isa 9:6, Isa 53:5, Mic 5:5)

- **Isa 9:6** 🔵 (✓) *target: Peace*
  > Isa 9:6 For to us a child is born , to us a son is given ; and the government shall be upon his shoulder , and his name shall be called Wonderful Counselor , Mighty God , Everlasting Father , Prince of Peace .
  - notes: Prince of Peace — shalom as the messianic king's title and identity.
- **Isa 53:5** 🔵 (✓) *target: peace*
  > Isa 53:5 But he was pierced for our transgressions ; he was crushed for our iniquities ; upon him was the chastisement that brought us peace , and with his wounds we are healed .
  - notes: Upon him was the chastisement that brought us peace — vicarious purchase of shalom through the Servant's suffering.
- **Mic 5:5** 🔵 (✓) *target: peace*
  > Mic 5:5 And he shall be their peace . When the Assyrian comes into our land and treads in our palaces , then we will raise against him seven shepherds and eight princes of men ;
  - notes: He shall be their peace — messianic ruler as shalom personified.
- **Psa 72:7** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Psa 72:7 In his days may the righteous flourish , and peace abound , till the moon be no more !
  - notes: Peace abound till the moon be no more — eschatological peace abounding in the messianic reign.
- **Psa 85:10** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Psa 85:10 Steadfast love and faithfulness meet ; righteousness and peace kiss each other.
  - notes: Righteousness and peace kiss each other — cosmic convergence of shalom and righteousness in the eschatological vision.
- **Isa 9:7** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Isa 9:7 Of the increase of his government and of peace there will be no end , on the throne of David and over his kingdom , to establish it and to uphold it with justice and with righteousness from this time forth and forevermore . The zeal of the Lord of hosts will do this .
  - notes: Of the increase of his government and peace there will be no end — endless shalom of the messianic reign.
- **Isa 32:18** (✓) *target: peaceful*
  > Isa 32:18 My people will abide in a peaceful habitation , in secure dwellings , and in quiet resting places .
  - notes: My people will abide in a peaceful habitation — eschatological condition of God's people at rest.
- **Isa 52:7** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Isa 52:7 How beautiful upon the mountains are the feet of him who brings good news , who publishes peace , who brings good news of happiness , who publishes salvation , who says to Zion , “ Your God reigns .”
  - notes: Herald bringing good news who publishes peace — shalom as content of the gospel announcement.
- **Isa 55:12** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Isa 55:12 “For you shall go out in joy and be led forth in peace ; the mountains and the hills before you shall break forth into singing , and all the trees of the field shall clap their hands .
  - notes: Go out in joy and be led forth in peace — restoration as condition of inner peace.
- **Isa 60:17** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Isa 60:17 Instead of bronze I will bring gold , and instead of iron I will bring silver ; instead of wood , bronze , instead of stones , iron . I will make your overseers peace and your taskmasters righteousness .
  - notes: I will make your overseers peace — peace as the governing principle of the restored community.
- **Isa 66:12** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Isa 66:12 For thus says the Lord : “ Behold , I will extend peace to her like a river , and the glory of the nations like an overflowing stream ; and you shall nurse , you shall be carried upon her hip , and bounced upon her knees .
  - notes: I will extend peace like a river — overflowing eschatological peace.
- **Nah 1:15** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Nah 1:15 Behold , upon the mountains , the feet of him who brings good news , who publishes peace ! Keep your feasts , O Judah ; fulfill your vows , for never again shall the worthless pass through you; he is utterly cut off .
  - notes: Herald who publishes peace — parallel to Isa 52:7, messianic proclamation.
- **Zec 6:13** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Zec 6:13 It is he who shall build the temple of the Lord and shall bear royal honor , and shall sit and rule on his throne . And there shall be a priest on his throne , and the counsel of peace shall be between them both .”’
  - notes: Counsel of peace between messianic priest-king — peace characterising messianic governance.
- **Zec 8:12** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Zec 8:12 For there shall be a sowing of peace . The vine shall give its fruit , and the ground shall give its produce , and the heavens shall give their dew . And I will cause the remnant of this people to possess all these things .
  - notes: There shall be a sowing of peace — peace as the condition of the restored eschatological era.
- **Zec 9:10** (✓) *target: peace*
  > Zec 9:10 I will cut off the chariot from Ephraim and the war horse from Jerusalem ; and the battle bow shall be cut off , and he shall speak peace to the nations ; his rule shall be from sea to sea , and from the River to the ends of the earth .
  - notes: The messianic king shall speak peace to the nations — universal messianic proclamation.

### `H7965H` — 1/1 classified · 1 anchor verse(s)

**Group `406-001`** (1 verse — anchors: Judg 6:24)

- **Judg 6:24** 🔵 (✓) *target: Peace*
  > Judg 6:24 Then Gideon built an altar there to the Lord and called it, The Lord Is Peace . To this day it still stands at Ophrah , which belongs to the Abiezrites .
  - notes: Gideon built an altar and called it YHWH-Shalom (The Lord Is Peace) following the theophany of Judg 6:23. The divine name commemorates God as the source and substance of peace sealed in the altar after the inner-peace encounter (Peace be to you. Do not fear).

### `H7965I` — 46/46 classified · 3 anchor verse(s)

**Group `2509-001`** (13 verses — anchors: Psa 35:27, Jer 29:11)

- **Psa 35:27** 🔵 (✓) *target: welfare*
  > Psa 35:27 Let those who delight in my righteousness shout for joy and be glad and say evermore , “ Great is the Lord , who delights in the welfare of his servant !”
  - notes: Lord delights in the welfare of his servant — God's inner orientation toward his servant's comprehensive welfare; sha.lom as the object of divine delight.
- **Jer 29:11** 🔵 (✓) *target: welfare*
  > Jer 29:11 For I know the plans I have for you, declares the Lord , plans for welfare and not for evil , to give you a future and a hope .
  - notes: Plans for welfare and not for evil, to give you a future and a hope — divine purposive orientation toward the comprehensive welfare of his people.
- **Job 21:9** (✓) *target: safe*
  > Job 21:9 Their houses are safe from fear , and no rod of God is upon them .
  - notes: Houses safe from fear, no rod of God — the welfare-condition of the wicked observed; inner content: the absence of fear and divine discipline.
- **Psa 38:3** (✓) *target: health*
  > Psa 38:3 There is no soundness in my flesh because of your indignation ; there is no health in my bones because of my sin .
  - notes: No health in my bones because of sin — sha.lom-soundness absent as somatic consequence of sin; welfare/wholeness broken by inner disorder.
- **Psa 55:18** (✓) *target: safety*
  > Psa 55:18 He redeems my soul in safety from the battle that I wage , for many are arrayed against me .
  - notes: He redeems my soul in safety — sha.lom-safety as the condition of the soul (nephesh) under divine redemption.
- **Psa 72:3** (✓) *target: prosperity*
  > Psa 72:3 Let the mountains bear prosperity for the people , and the hills , in righteousness !
  - notes: Mountains bearing prosperity for the people — eschatological covenant welfare.
- **Psa 73:3** (✓) *target: prosperity*
  > Psa 73:3 For I was envious of the arrogant when I saw the prosperity of the wicked .
  - notes: Psalmist envious of the arrogant when he saw the prosperity of the wicked — inner-being engagement through envy provoked by observing sha.lom-prosperity.
- **Isa 38:17** (✓) *target: welfare*
  > Isa 38:17 Behold , it was for my welfare that I had great bitterness ; but in love you have delivered my life from the pit of destruction , for you have cast all my sins behind your back .
  - notes: For my welfare I had great bitterness; in love you delivered my life — sha.lom achieved paradoxically through suffering and divine love.
- **Isa 45:7** (✓) *target: well-being*
  > Isa 45:7 I form light and create darkness , I make well-being and create calamity ; I am the Lord , who does all these things .
  - notes: I make well-being and create calamity — God as sovereign creator of sha.lom and its opposite; comprehensive welfare as divine creation.
- **Jer 29:7** (✓) *target: welfare*
  > Jer 29:7 But seek the welfare of the city where I have sent you into exile , and pray to the Lord on its behalf , for in its welfare you will find your welfare .
  - notes: Seek the welfare of the city; in its welfare you will find your welfare — active orientation toward sha.lom; welfare is participatory and shared.
- **Jer 33:6** (✓) *target: prosperity*
  > Jer 33:6 Behold , I will bring to it health and healing , and I will heal them and reveal to them abundance of prosperity and security .
  - notes: I will reveal to them abundance of prosperity and security — God revealing sha.lom-prosperity.
- **Jer 33:9** (✓) *target: prosperity*
  > Jer 33:9 And this city shall be to me a name of joy , a praise and a glory before all the nations of the earth who shall hear of all the good that I do for them. They shall fear and tremble because of all the good and all the prosperity I provide for it .
  - notes: All the prosperity I provide for it — God providing sha.lom-prosperity for Jerusalem.
- **Jer 38:4** (✓) *target: welfare*
  > Jer 38:4 Then the officials said to the king , “ Let this man be put to death , for he is weakening the hands of the soldiers who are left in this city , and the hands of all the people , by speaking such words to them. For this man is not seeking the welfare of this people , but their harm .”
  - notes: This man is not seeking the welfare of this people, but their harm — inner orientation of seeking sha.lom contrasted with seeking harm.

**Group `2509-002`** (4 verses — anchors: Deu 29:19)

- **Deu 29:19** 🔵 (✓) *target: safe*
  > Deu 29:19 one who, when he hears the words of this sworn covenant , blesses himself in his heart , saying , ‘I shall be safe , though I walk in the stubbornness of my heart .’ This will lead to the sweeping away of moist and dry alike.
  - notes: Blesses himself in his heart saying 'I shall be safe' while walking in stubbornness of heart — sha.lom claimed by the self-deceived heart; the false inner assurance of welfare accompanying covenant violation.
- **Job 15:21** (✓) *target: prosperity*
  > Job 15:21 Dreadful sounds are in his ears ; in prosperity the destroyer will come upon him .
  - notes: In prosperity the destroyer will come — sha.lom-prosperity as the illusory condition of the wicked before destruction.
- **Jer 4:10** (✓) *target: well*
  > Jer 4:10 Then I said , “ Ah , Lord God , surely you have utterly deceived this people and Jerusalem , saying , ‘It shall be well with you,’ whereas the sword has reached their very life .”
  - notes: Prophets said 'It shall be well with you' while the sword reached their very life (nephesh) — false promise of welfare reaching the inner person.
- **Jer 23:17** (✓) *target: well*
  > Jer 23:17 They say continually to those who despise the word of the Lord , ‘It shall be well with you’; and to everyone who stubbornly follows his own heart , they say , ‘ No disaster shall come upon you.’”
  - notes: It shall be well with you to everyone who stubbornly follows his own heart — false welfare promise to the stubborn-hearted; parallel to Deu 29:19.

### `H7965J` — 5/5 classified · 1 anchor verse(s)

- **1Ch 12:17** 🔵 (✓) *target: friendship*
  > 1Ch 12:17 David went out to meet them and said to them, “ If you have come to me in friendship to help me, my heart will be joined to you; but if to betray me to my adversaries , although there is no wrong in my hands , then may the God of our fathers see and rebuke you.”
  - notes: If you have come to me in friendship (sha.lom) to help me, my heart will be joined to you — sha.lom as inner relational loyalty directly connected to heart-union.

  > Psa 41:9 Even my close friend in whom I trusted , who ate my bread , has lifted his heel against me.
  - notes: My close friend (ish sha.lom) in whom I trusted — sha.lom names the bond of friendship whose betrayal is devastating.

  > Psa 55:20 My companion stretched out his hand against his friends ; he violated his covenant .
  - notes: Stretched out his hand against his friends (sha.lom); he violated his covenant — sha.lom friendship violated alongside covenant.
- **Jer 20:10** (✓) *target: close*
  > Jer 20:10 For I hear many whispering . Terror is on every side ! “ Denounce him! Let us denounce him!” say all my close friends , watching for my fall . “ Perhaps he will be deceived ; then we can overcome him and take our revenge on him .”
  - notes: All my close friends (anshei sha.lom), watching for my fall — men of sha.lom who are secretly hostile.

  > Jer 38:22 Behold , all the women left in the house of the king of Judah were being led out to the officials of the king of Babylon and were saying , “‘Your trusted friends have deceived you and prevailed against you; now that your feet are sunk in the mud , they turn away from you.’
